msg:Traveling with my mother-in-law and children, I chose Moutai Boutique Hotel. Moutai Resort has four hotels, Boutique, Classic, Treasure and Premium. Boutique and Classic are next to each other. They are basic hotels. Treasure is medium and Premium is high-end. I stayed for a total of five nights, all in Boutique, but all facilities in the hotel are shared, and the people in the reservation depar**ent are also very professional. Before check-in, they said they would help me upgrade to Classic, but because I read the comments that Classic would be noisy, I still chose to stay in Boutique. They cleaned every day. The hotel has a gym, swimming pool and self-service laundry room. The room is also large. The central air-conditioning does not need to be plugged in to get electricity. Sometimes the air-conditioning is not turned on in the evening, but it is not hot at the end of April. I have also experienced the Chinese restaurant. The resort has three swimming pools, two indoors and one outdoor. Opposite is a beach. The set meal also includes free afternoon tea. The Chinese restaurant tastes good, with Cantonese, Hunan and Guizhou cuisines, etc. The overall experience is very good. The free travel photography was quite speechless. I stayed for two nights after staying for three nights, so I got two free travel photography. My mother-in-law took the photos for the first time, and I took the photos for the second time. The photos were free, but the selection and retouching were charged. My mother-in-law spent more than 300 yuan. I also went to take the photos. The photographer was very good and took good care of the guests in the hot weather. The woman who selected the photos was quite fierce. I thought the style of the photos was very old, so I only selected 5 free photos. When she saw that I didn't want to choose more, she said, "Please choose faster, there are guests behind me." I didn't choose more for the last photo, but I couldn't resist her eloquence. I spent 100 yuan more to buy her refined photos. After taking the photos, she refined more than 20 photos 10 minutes later. What can I say? The photos were retouched on the assembly line, and the layers and filters were changed. Finally, based on their retouching, I retouched them myself. The overall experience is good for the photographer, but bad for the selection of photos. She said they also had performance pressure, so my mother-in-law had to give her a good review. I think itâ€™s okay to spend one or two hundred yuan on a travel photo shoot, but when I got home today, I still told this story for your reference. Hahahaha, the other service staff in the hotel are super nice!!! I will choose this hotel again when I go to Sanya next time! Maotai Group is rising!

The dinner buffet is delicious and very worthwhile. There are rich and delicious varieties. There are also brothers and sisters singing live, which is very a**ospheric.
